$CALL_SERVICE: tab_fte.cfg => tab_fte_table (request:HR_LHEP_10210)
SQL: [SQL]

SQL: [SQL]:select sotr.person_id, sotr.tab_n, sotr.F, sotr.I, sotr.O, sotr.FIO, sotr.otdel, sotr.post , sotr.division, sotr.category, sotr.usl_truda, sotr.shtat_direct, oklad.oklad, FTE.thema, oklad.personal_nadbav , oklad.oklad+oklad.personal_nadbav itogo , (1+oklad.personal_nadbav)/(oklad.oklad-oklad.personal_nadbav) fte from sotrudniki sotr left join oklad on sotr.tab_n=oklad.tab_n left join FTE on sotr.person_id=FTE.person_id where lab_id = 100000 order by sotr.FIO Processed in 81ms.
NumTableRows=200;
